Our catalog with **#20250419** (Catalog version **3.4.330** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **41** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **484** products of **296** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **643** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

!

> 4.5.0 NEW FEATURES as.integer(rl) and hence as.raw(rl) now work for a list of raw(1) elements, as proposed by Michael Chirico's PR#18696. graphics' grid() gains optional argument nintLog. New functions check\_package\_urls() and check\_package\_dois() in package tools for checking URLs and DOIs in package sources.

> 2.84.6 (April 16, 2025) [stable] NEW: If the org create scratch command times out before the scratch org is ready, you run the org resume scratch command to poll for completion and see the results. You can now specify how long the command waits before it returns control of the terminal to you with the new --wait flag; the output shows the progress of the scratch org create. Previously you had to keep running the org resume scratch command until the scratch org was ready. In this example the command waits for 10 minutes before returning control to you:
